    commands[command]
        ? commands[command](e)
        : _runCallbackFromString( command, e)
}

    var _fn = FORTUNA.UTILS.getFnFromString(methodName, FORTUNA.UI)

    _fn && _fn(e)
}

				odds.push(44650466);

				tm.releaseOtherBetItems(odds);
			}
	}, true );
</script><script type="text/javascript">
				FORTUNA.run ( function () {
					var tm = FORTUNA.UI.ticketManager;
					if ( tm ) { tm.initTicket(); }
				}, true);
			</script>
			</div><div id="ticket-ajax-indicator"></div><div id="drop-zones-holder"></div>
